 Border security forces personnel have caught an empty boat flowing into the Ravi river in Amritsar district of Punjab
 isse do din pehle bhi tatarakshak balon ne gujarat tat ke nikat ek pakistani naav pakadi thi
 The boat has been caught in the Parrot Post area of amritsar district
 seemaa suraksha bal ke mahanideshak ke ke sharma ne dilli main kaha, naav main koi bhi sandigdh vastu nahin mili he or praathmik jaanch main lagata he ki yah naav bahakar bharat kii ore aa gai thi
 It is noteworthy that this Pakistani boat has been caught at a time when the border surveillance has been tightened due to increasing tension between India and Pakistan

 desh main bank acount khulwaane ke liye aapako apni photograph ke saath ek pahchaan patr or ek adress pruf lagaana anivaary he
 These documents are called Reserve Bank KYC (no Your Customer) documents
 iske alaava mobile or internet conection, alpiji conection, hotel main thaharne jaisi tamaam sevaaon ke liye bhi aapako inhen documents kii jarurat padati he

 What are KYC documents According to the central government's instructions, you can use 6 types of documents to open a bank account
 in documents ke jariye bank aapaki pahchaan sunishchit karata he
 For all such services along with bank account, you need to photocopy these documents
 in documents kii photocopy ko aap aamtaur par self atest karte hue istemaal karte hai
 After which your unique bank account opens and you get other services like mobile sim
 ye documents he- passport, driving license, voter idi card, pan card, aadhaar card or naregaa job card
 Use caution in using KYC documents Caution: If you are using any of your KYC documents for taking any service or facility including bank account, then you need to take some precautions
 - kisi surat main apana kevaisi document kisi duusare vyakti ko istemaal karne ke liye na den
 The use of your document by someone you know is also fraudulent
 pakade jane kii sthiti main sajaa ke praavdhaan hai
 At the same time, the use of your document by others can cause big losses for you in the future
 - kisi bhi suvidha ko lene ke liye jab apane kevaisi document kaa photocopy lagaaein to us photocopy main disclimur jarur daalen
 If you are using a document for a mobile SIM, then write clearly on the photocopy that the date on which the photocopy is being used to get the mobile SIM from which company
 is disclimur ke neeche hi aap document ko atest karen
 - Always give your KYC document to be photocopied in front of you
 photocopy kii dukaan par saavdhaanee barte ki kahin koi aapke document kii atirikt copy to nahin nikaal rahaa he
 Even if there is no clear image of any document while doing photocopying, then destroy it from the shopkeeper so that it cannot be used by any other person
 gauratlab he kiapake kevaisi document kaa koi vyakti galat istemaal kar saktaa he
 He can open a bank account or take a loan from a bank along with getting his passport based on your document
 aise maamalon main farji document se hui deal ke kanoon paksh main aap jimmedaar honge
 On the other hand, if it has been used for banking and loans, then financial losses may also be incurred

 vahiin 23 varsh pehle yuvati kaa janm hua tha

 Actually, the last date for depositing the first installment of advance tax is 15 June
 isliye tex vibhaag tamaam karadaataaon ko is babat sandesh bhejtaa he
 But here it is important to know that which taxpayers are required to fill the advance tax? How much tax is paid and when? In this report, with the help of Chartered Accountant Ankit Gupta, we are answering all the questions related to advance tax
 kya hota he advance tex?iskar kanoon, 1961 kii dhara 208 ke tahat har vyaktigat karadaata jinaki maujuuda vitt varsh ke liye salanaa tex dendaree 10,000 rupye se zyada hoti he unke liye advance tex bharna jaruri hota he
 This includes merchants, professionals or taxpayers who have income from multiple sources
 april se june ke dauraan aapaki jo bhi aay hui he, us aay par aap yah tex bharte hai
 Keep in mind that if you are a jobber and your accounts department is deducting income tax from your salary every month, then be assured that your tax liability is being met on time
 lekin agar vetan ke alaava share, mutual fund, property yaa kisi anya strot se aapaki aay ho rahi he to us par aapako advance tex dena hoga
 When do you have to pay advance tax? According to the Income Tax Act, individual taxpayers can pay their advance tax in four installments
 ye chaar taarikh har saal kii 15 june, 15 sitambar, 15 disambar or 15 march hoti he
 You have to pay 15% by 15 June, 45% by 15 September, 75% by 15 December and full tax by 15 March
 samay par bhugtan na karne par dendaree par prati maah ek fisadi kii dar se byaaj dena hota he
 How will the tax be collected? Let's take the example of the first installment, which a taxpayer has to submit by June 15
 sabase pehle april se june ke dauraan hui aay ko jodie
 After this, calculate your tax liability on the basis of savings
 yah gananaa aap online inakam tex vibhaag kii website par bhi kar sakate hai
 After calculation you can collect advance tax either online or offline

 HDFC Bank, ICICI Bank has started levying a minimum fee of Rs 150 on deposits or withdrawals more than four times in a month
 exis bank ne bhi isi tarah kaa kadam uthaaya he
 HDFC Bank said in a circular that this fee will be charged on savings as well as salary accounts
 yah buudhvaar se prabhaav main aa gaya
 According to the circular, HDFC Bank also fixed a cash transaction limit of Rs 25,000 per day for third parties
 iske alaava nakad rakrakhaav shulk waapas liya jayega
 All of them have come into effect since Wednesday
 is kadam ko nakad len-dein ko hatotsahit karne tathaa digital bhugtan abhiyaan ko gati dene ke kadam ke rup main dekha ja rahaa he
 For accounts with zero deposits, the limit of free cash withdrawal will continue up to four times and there will be no charge on cash deposits
 isiaisiai bank ke maamle main shulk vahi rahenge jo 8 november ko notebandi kii ghoshnaa se pehle thi
 In some other cases such charges have been increased
 isiaisiai bank kii website ke anusaar mul shakha (jahaan khataadharaka kaa khaataa he) main ek ek maheene main pehle chaar len-dein ke liye koi shulk nahin lagegaa
 Thereafter a fee of Rs 5 per Rs 1,000 will be levied
 yah samaan maheene ke liye nunatam 150 rupee hoga
 In the case of third parties the limit will be Rs 50,000 per day
 mul shakha ke alaava anya shakhaon ke maamle main isiaisiai bank ek maheene main pehali nakad nikasi ke liye koi shulk nahin legaa
 But after that Rs 5 per 1,000 will be charged
 iske liye nunatam shulk 150 rupee rakhaa gaya he
 The comments kahin bhi nakad jamaa ke liye isiaisiai bank 5 rupee prati hajaar (nunatam 150 rupee) shulk legaa
 At the same time, cash deposit will be free for the first time in a month in a machine that accepts cash, and after that a fee of Rs 5 per 1,000 will be charged
 exis bank main pehle paanch len-dein yaa 10 lakh rupye nakad jamaa yaa nikasi muft hogi
 After that Rs 5 per Rs 1,000 or Rs 150 fee whichever is higher
 abhi yah pataa nahin chalaa he ki kya saarvajanik kshetra ke bainkon ne bhi isi prakaar kaa koi kadam uthaaya he
 When contacted, a senior official said that the banks have not received any instructions from the government in this regard

 ) The Delhi Parents Association is constantly receiving complaints from parents that their children are carrying an excessive burden under pressure
 in shikayaton ke aadhaar par mangalvaar ko dilli parents association kii team ne School Bag Weight reality check kiya
 In many places outside Delhi's streets, members of the association with parents weighed the bags, which revealed that the children were carrying more weight than the prescribed standards
 ye reality check mohan garden ilaake main kiya gaya
 Aparajita Gautam, president of the Delhi Parents Association, told Aaj Tak that they collected bag sample data of 86 children from nursery to 11th
 in bacchon ke bag kaa vajan mapa gaya
 He said that if that data is studied, only 1 child bag out of 86 weighs as per rules while the rest 85 kids bags weigh 3 times the standard
 sample collection main udhaaharan dekhen to class 2 ke bachche ke bag kaa ausatan vajan 5 kilo tha
 Whereas as per rules it should be up to one and a half kilos
 yahaan tak ki nursery or prepe ke bacchon ke bag kaa ausatan vajan 4
 Turned out to be 5 kilos
 aparajita kaa kahana he ki yahaan ye baat dhyaan dene kii he ki skool khatm hone ke baad ye vajan liya gaya gaya tha, yadi subah ye vajan liya gaya hota to 1 kilo (khaane ke dibbe or pani kii bottle) vajan or jud jaataa jo ki amuman har din bachche uthaate hi hai
 The Madras High Court, Delhi High Court and various departments (DOE, CBSE, MHRD) gave several orders, according to which the weight of the subject, books and bags has been determined according to the class of school children
 vajah ye he ki bag ke baari vajan ke chalate bacchon kii ridh kii haddi par uskaa khatarnaak prabhaav pad rahaa he
 The Delhi Parents Association thanked the parents of Kamal Model School, who participated extensively in this program
 dilli shiksha vibhaag dwaara 29 november 2018 ko jari circular main bhi class ke hisaab se vajan maapdand tay kiya gaya
